 In Maharashtra, the Congress and the Nationalist Congress Party (NCP) are trying to beat the BJP in the 2019 Lok Sabha elections, but the seat tussle between the two parties is still stuck
 ensipi netaa ajit pavaar ne kaha ki maharashtra main 48 loksabhaa siton main se 8 ko lekar congress ke saath baatcheet puri nahin ho saki he
 While the remaining 40 seats have been mutually agreed
 bataa den ki congress or ensipi ne aagaamee loksabhaa chunaav main maharashtra main bijepi kaa saamana karne ke liye samaan vichaardhaara vaale dalon ke saath gathbandhan karne kaa faisla kiya he
 However, the sheet sharing formula has not yet been decided between the two parties
 soobe kii 48 siton main abhi tay nahin he ki ensipi or congress kitni-kitni siton par chunaav ladengi

 in siton main pune or ahmednagar seat bhi shaamil he

 Which will be Thursday
 sawan kii shivaratri kab he-sawan kii shivaratri kaa hindu dharm main vishesh mahatv bataaya gaya he
 According to beliefs, Bholenath is pleased and fulfills wishes by offering water to Lord Shiva on the day of Shivaratri
 is baar sawan kii shivaratri 30 july ko pad rahi he
 That day is Tuesday
 is din log shivlinga par belptr or datura chadhaate hai
 Auspicious time of worship on the day of Shivratri - Auspicious time of worship on Shivaratri in the morning 9
 10 se dopaher 2 baje tak rahegaa
 However, according to astrologers, the entire day of Shivaratri is extremely auspicious for worship
 bhakt is din bhagwaan shiv kii puja archana kisi bhi samay kar sakate hai
 12 Shivaratri falls every year - 12 Shivaratris come every year for the devotees of Lord Shiva, which falls on every Trayodashi
 shivaratri ke din log upwas rakhkar bhagwaan shankar kii puja archana karte hai
 It is believed that if a virgin girl observes Shivaratri fast, she gets a desired groom
 phalgun main padane vaali shivaratri ko mahashivaratri ke rup main puja jaataa he
 It is believed that on this day Shiva Parvati was married
 shivaratri par bhagwaan shiv kaa aise karen abhishek-shivaratri ke din subah jaldi uthakar snaan kar len
 While going to the temple take water, milk, curd, honey, ghee, sugar, perfume, sandalwood, saffron, hemp together in a vessel and anoint the Shivalinga
 bhagwaan shiv ko lagaaein in chizon kaa bhoga--shiv ko genhun se bani chijen arpit karne se aap unhen jaldi prasann kar sakate hai-mana jaataa he ki eshwarya paane ke liye shiv ko mung kaa bhoga lagaaya janaa chahie
 - By offering sesame to Shiv, sins are destroyed
 aazaadee ke ikhattar saal baad aaj jab ham phir yah charchaa kar rahe hai ki swatantraaa or swaittata kaa, usul or amal donon ke lihaaj se, hamaare liye kya matlab he, tab shaayad is sachaai kii yaad dilaanaa jaruri he ki adhikaar or jimmedaariyaan saath-saath chalati hai
 In this light, we would like to see how those rights and responsibilities are seen in the doctor-patient relationship
 in donon ke bich aapasi vyavhaar kaa arth doctor or client se zyada kaa he
 It also gives a glimpse of the larger society and legal influences which will inevitably affect their mutual functioning as well
 isliye clinics main mulaakaat ke vakt marij ke dimag main swaittata kaa jo ehsaas hota he, vah is baat se tay hoga ki doctor ko samaaj kis tarah dekhtaa he
 Similarly, the sense of immediate importance in the mind of a doctor, whether shared or unilateral, is also affected by many things including law
 aadhunik samaaj shaayad do baton ke bich dolata rahata he
 On the one hand, he considers the medical profession to be an auspicious of all wisdom and care and hopes that he will explain everything from road rage to global warming and will always work with selfless devotion and dedication
 duusari taraf, vah chikitsa ke peshey ko paisa banane or jhapatmari ke aujaar ke taur par bhi dekhtaa he, jo beemaari or takalif donon kaa beja phayda uthaa rahaa he
 In return, the profession of medicine also appears to be swinging badly between very different approaches
 ek str par viraasat main mila paropkaaree, maanavtaavaadi rukh he, jisamen doctor khud ko tamaam jaruratmandon, khaskar garibon or saadhanheenon, kii dekhbhaal or sahaayta karne ke ferj se bandhe shaks ke taur par dekhtaa he, to duusare str par dhan-daulat kaa pralobhan he
 The fact is that most of the medical care in India is actually in the private sector and that insurance is a very small part of the healthcare provided by medical insurance or employer money
 lihaaja swasthya seva kii zyaadaatar laagtein aakhirkaar "boote se baahar jaakar kiye gaye'' kharchon ko uthaani padati hai
 The theater of this care is mainly clinics, nursing homes and large and small hospitals spread across the country
 iskaa doosraa hissaa yah he ki medical practice ke liye prabhavi niyam-kaayade vaaki nadaarad hai
 The Medical Regulatory Council of India (MCI), the main regulatory body of medicine, has done hardly any praise
 chikitsa ke peshewar sangh, britain ke ulat, na to niamak kii bhoomika main hai or na hi ve license dene vaale adhikari hai
 So a UK psychiatrist is a licensee of the Royal College of Psychiatry, but in India, the Indian Psychiatry Society does not license a psychiatrist, gives MCI
 isliye peshewar sansthaaen siforishein kar sakati hai, practice ke disha-nirdesh bana sakati hai, or yah sachmuch unka kaam bhi he, par unka kaam to sadasyon ke hiton kii chintaa karnaa bhi he
 This goal, that is, the interest of the practicing doctors and the interest of the society that the doctors treat, is of course not always the same
 lihaaja in donon ko jodna yakeenan jahaan sabase ahm kaam he, vahiin sawaal yah he ki yah kitne asardaar dhang se hota he
 It is also important to remember that a doctor does not need to register with professional associations to practice as a specialist in the country
 emsiai kaa registration hi kaaphi he
 In this scenario, the rules of practice are often left to the practicing doctor
 sach yah he ki medical practice nirvivaad rup se aam taur par acchhee hi he
 a large number of doctors will work only with the well being of the patient in mind and the patient who gives his health and his confidence in the care of the doctor
 yah bhi itnaa hi saaf ho gaya he ki kabhi-kabhi yah bharosa galat sabit hoga
 Unnecessary scrutiny orders will be given, unnecessary procedures will be written, cut-practice means commissioning in investigation and referral
 kuch prescripshan ataarkik honge
 These examples of the richness of the medical profession have pushed a large part of the practice being practiced with great difficulty into difficult light in one sense
 medical kadachaar ko lekar badhati chintaaen or saath hi adaalatein or samaaj bhi jis tarah medical practice ko lekar aalochanatmak ravaiya apana rahi he, ye shaayad isi taraf ishaara karte hai
 They also reflect a growing pessimistic feeling
 yah ek lihaaj se samaaj ke jhagadalupan ke badhate str kaa sanket he or duusare str par yah is baat kii samaj he ki kisi bhi peshey ko jis tarah khud ko niyam-kaayadon se baandhna chahie, vah shaayad hota dikhaai nahin de rahaa he
 Today, when we have had many discussions about what freedom and autonomy mean, it may also be good to consider what kind of discussion and debates the medical community relies on
 manochikitsa ke anushaasan main is charchaa kii ahmiyat or bhi bad jaati he kyonki yah vah anushaasan he jisamen samaaj kii nirmitiyaan prabhaavshaalee hai
 Mental health law is particularly an example of this
 is sambhaavna par vichaar karne kii darkaar he ki kuch logon ko kisi vakt—apane maansik vikaar kii vajah se—kam yaa lambey vakt ke liye "anaichhik'' yaa "samarthit'' ilaaj kii jarurat ho sakati he
 These rules and reluctance are the heart of the mental health law protecting the rights of the person while undergoing treatment
 saath hi, yah kab tay hoga ki isaki jarurat he, koun yah tay karegaa—doctor, parivaar, adaalat yaa samiti—ye hadbandiyaan aise mudde hai jinase tamaam samaajon ko nipatna padataa he
 Another example is the very intriguing concept called "advance directive" in psychiatry
 isamen vyakti sulajhepan or sehatmandi kii haalat main yah tay karata he ki sambhavit bhavi naakaaraapan kii haalat main uske saath kya kiya or kya nahin kiya ja saktaa he
 So this means that i am saying that if i get sick from some mental disease, then i decide how my treatment will be
 alabatta asal vyavhaar main yah kai dilachasp or pechida sawaal paidaa karata he—koun-sa swa nirnay lene vaala swa he, ek swa duusare ke liye kaise tay kar saktaa he, ise kab radd kiya ja saktaa he, or yah tathy ki jab ham ise vyakti, doctor or kanoon ke bich titarafa qaraar main badal dete hai; tab kya hota he, is par charchaa kaa ab bhi intjaar he
 Alok Sareen is a Consultant Psychiatrist at Sitaram Bhartia Institute of Science and Research, New Delhi
 mumbai ke varsova main ek building ke swimming pool main duubakar 20 saal ke yuvak kii maut ho gai
 Police are considering this death as just an accident
 par yuvak ke gharavaale hatya ke peeche sajeesh kaa ashanka jataa rahe hai
 He was also friends with the young man during the drowning
 20 saal kaa imran shaikh kii mangalvaar raat varsova ke swimming pool main doobane se maut ho gai
 Imran went for a swim in this swimming pool with his friends
 police ke mutabir imran kii maut ek haadasa he
 While the family members of Imran are calling his death a conspiracy
 police ke mutabik varsova ke woodstak building ke is swimming pool main imran ke saath uskaa ek dost muddasar or do ladkiyaan thim or in sabhi ne jamkar sharaab pi rakhi thi
 Why did not Emraan's companions try to save him
 police is sawaal kaa jawaab talash rahi he
 The three companions have been arrested by the police on charges of negligence
 saath hi police gharavaalon ke aaropon kii jaanch bhi kar rahi he
 Samajwadi Party President Akhilesh Yadav said about the Congress and the bjp's alliance for the assembly elections in Madhya Pradesh later this year, that the Congress is responsible for how people of an ideology come together
 akhilesh yadav ne shanivaar ko madhya pradesh ke daure par shadol main pradesh main congress ke saath gathbandhan ke sawaal par yah baat kahi
 Former Uttar Pradesh Chief Minister Akhilesh Yadav said that SP and Godwana Ganatantra Party (GGP) will fight assembly elections in Madhya Pradesh
 pichley chunaav main jin ilaakon main sapa kaa vot acha rahaa he, vahaan sapa ladegi
 The opposition camp does not seem to be one
 bispi pramukh mayawati ne pehle hi madhya pradesh main alag se chunaav ladane kaa elaan kar chuki hai
 Despite all efforts at the national level, the opposition camp does not seem ready to unite
 gathbandhan ko taiyaar congresis bich congress kii ore se yah jarur kaha gaya he ki party 2019 ke aam chunaavon ke liye samaan vichaardhaara vaale dalon ke saath gathbandhan karegi or satta main lautegi
 Senior Congress leader Priyanka Chaturvedi said on Friday that her party would not compromise ideology and values
 party kii rashtriya pravaktaa chaturvedi ne kaha, ham sirf gathbandhan karne ke liye apni vichaardhaara or mulyon ke saath samjhauta karne ke liye baadhya nahin hai
 We will approach all opposition political parties, a coalition will be formed on the basis of our understanding
 bataa den ki madhya pradesh vidhansabha kii 230 siton ke liye isi saal november-disambar main chunaav hone hai
 At present, the main contest in most of the seats of the state is between the BJP and the Congress
 yahaan 2003 se bijepi kii sarkaar he or isse pehle 10 saal tak congress ne raaj kiya tha
 In the 2013 assembly elections, BJP formed the government by winning 165 seats out of a total of 230 assembly seats
 congress 58 siton tak simat gai thi
 While the BSP won 4 seats and others won 3 seats
 Vodafone Idea ke marjar ke baad bhi nai company ko bazaar main kaaphi pratispardhaa kaa saamana karnaa pad rahaa he
 However, the company has still not given up and is making all efforts to stay in the market
 postped or preeped donon hi graahakon ko adishan benifits die ja rahe hai
 Now the company has come up with a new plan for new smartphone customers
 nayaa ofer samsung Galaxy S10 graahakon ke liye pesh kiya gaya he
 Vodafone has partnered with Samsung and offers prepaid and postpaid customers
 haalanki har baar kii tarah postped graahakon ko preeped graahakon kii tulana main atirikt phaayde die ja rahe hai

 postped graahakon ke liye:vodafone ke postped graahakon ko samsung gallexi S10 siries smartfones kharidne par 6,000 rupee kii vailu kaa netflix kaa 1 saal kaa free sabsakripshan milegaa
 This offer will be applicable to all S10 models - Galaxy S10e, Galaxy S10 and Galaxy S10 +
 nae divaais ko lene ke baad vodaphone postped graahakon ko is ofer ko actevet karne ke liye code- MYVODA milegaa
 The thing to keep in mind is that this offer is only for postpaid users and to activate this offer, customers should have a plan of at least Rs 499 or more
 iske liye alaava graahak ye bhi dhyaan rakhen ki ye ofer mybodaphone ap se actevet karne ke baad 72 ghante ke baad actevet hoga

 haalanki vodaphone kii ore se in graahakon ko kuch alag ofer diya ja rahaa he

 is sabsakripshan ke tahat graahakon ko 365 dinon kii validity ke saath roj 2GB data diya jayega
 Apart from this, customers will also get the benefit of unlimited local, STD and roaming calls
 ye ofer idia ke graahakon ke liye bhi he

 darrsal, apane aakhri bajet main siddharmaiya ne film city mysore main banaae jane kaa elaan kiya tha

 jise lekar siddharmaiya ne is par naaraazgi jaahir kii he or is par punarvichaar karne ko kaha he

 Winter - Rainfall in winter is due to west disturbance or jet stream in the plains of North India
 - jaade ke dinon main (janvari-farvari) tamilnadu ke taton par varsha lautate hue monsoon yaa uttari purvi monsoon ke kaaran hoti he
 2
 greeshm ritu- is ritu main assam or pashchim bengal rajyon main teevr ardra hawaaen chalane lagati hai, jinase garaj ke saath varsha ho jaati he
 - These winds are known as Narvester in Eastern India and Kaal Vaishakhi in Bengal
 - karnataka main inhen cheri blasm kaha jaataa he jo coffee kii krishi ke liye laabhadaayak he
 - Being profitable for mango crop, it is also called mango rain or mango shower in South India
 - uttar pashchim bharat ke shushk bhaagon main greeshm ritu main chalane vaali garm or shushk hawaaon ko“lu”kaha jaataa he
 3
 varsha ritu- is ritu main uttar pashchim bharat or pakistan main ushnadab kaa kshetra ban jaataa he, jise monsoon gart kehete hai
 At the same time, the Northern Thermal Convergence (NITC) begins to shift northward, causing the equatorial linear westerly wind and southeast commercial wind of the southern hemisphere to cross the equator and flow into India following Ferrell's law, which Also known as Southwest Monsoon
 - bharat kii zyaadaatar varsha ( lagbhag 80 fisadi) isi monsoon main hoti he
 - Due to the peninsular shape of India, the southwest monsoon is divided into two branches
 1
 Arabian Sea branch - Arabian Sea branch monsoon first comes in the first week of June in the state of Kerala, India
 - yahaan yah pashchimi ghat parvat se takaraa kar kerala ke taton par varsha karata he
 This is called monsoon blast
 - monsoon dwaara laai gai kuch ardrata kaa 65 fisadi bhaag arab sagar se aata he
 - a branch of the Arabian oceanic monsoon extends beyond the delta region of Sindh Nandi, through the desert of Rajasthan and directly hits the Himalayan Mountains and hence there is more rainfall around Dharamshala
 - rajasthan main sagariya monsoon maarg main avrodh na hone ke kaaran varsha kaa abhaav paaya jaataa he kyunki aravali parvat maala iske saamanantar padati he
 2
 bengal kii khadi kii shakha- gaaro, khaasi or jayantiya pahadiyon par bengal kii khadi se aane vaali hawaaen adhik varsha laati hai, jisaki vajah se yahaan sthit meghalaya vishwa main sabase zyada varsha praapt karne vaala sthaan he
 35% of the humidity brought by the monsoon comes from the Bay of Bengal
 - monsoon kii arab shakha tulanaatmak rup se adhik shaktishaalee hoti he
 4
 sharad ritu- is ritu ko monsoon prayaavartan kaa kaal (retreating monsoon sijan) kaha jaataa he
 - Tropical cyclones originate in the Bay of Bengal and the Arabian Sea in this season
 - in chakravaaton se odisha, andhra pradesh or pashchimi tateey kshetra main gujarat main kaaphi kshati pahunchati he
 Angered by the break-up of the Grand Alliance in Bihar, former JDU president and party MP Sharad Yadav appeared to the media for the first time
 sharad yadav ne kaha ki bihar janata ne hamen bijepi ke saath aane ke liye janadesh nahin diya tha
 He said that he regretted breaking the alliance
 bihar main lalu yadav kii argedy kaa saath chhod nitish kumaar ne bijepi ke saath sarkaar bana lee he jiske baad se party ke varisht netaa sharad yadav naaraaz bataae ja rahe hai
 There were reports of split in JDU after the break-up of the alliance
 party ke rajyasabha saansad ali anwar bhi nitish kumaar ke faisle se naaraaz hai

 lekin kisi bhi tarah kii jaan kii haani is ghatana main nahin hui yah ek acchhee khabar he

 aag itani bhanyakar thi ki isamen anye duusare saat vaahanon ko bhi nuksaan pahunchaa

 aag par kaabo paane main damakal adhikariyon ko aadhe ghante kaa samay lag gaya

 bataaya ja rahaa he ki iske prabhaav main aane vaala vyakti ashakt ho jayega jisase uski hinsak gatividhi ko rokna or use hiraasat main lenaa aasaan ho jayega

 unke pita govindrav pavaar baraamati ke krishak sahakaari sangh main kaam karte the or unki mata sharadabai pavaar, katewadi main parivaar ke kaam kii dekh-rekh karti thim
